## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillatory mechanics
**Analysis**: This task models the acceleration of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator, governed by Newton's second law where the net force depends nonlinearly on position x and/or velocity v, with possible explicit time-dependent driving forces.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Linear restoring force: dv_dt = c0 * x (simple harmonic oscillator)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear damping + linear restoring)
- Duffing oscillator (undriven): dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + linear damping)
- Driven Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (cubic restoring + damping + harmonic drive)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v (nonlinear damping)
- Driven van der Pol: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * x**2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t) (nonlinear damping + drive)
- Pendulum-like: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) (sinusoidal restoring force)
- Damped pendulum with drive: dv_dt = c0 * sin(c1 * x) + c2 * v + c3 * cos(c4 * t)
- Quintic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order nonlinearity)
- Quadratic-cubic restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (asymmetric potential)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * Abs(v) (quadratic velocity damping)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) + c2 * x (time-modulated stiffness)
- Rayleigh oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (cubic velocity nonlinearity)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope вҶ’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects вҶ’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay вҶ’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior вҶ’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects вҶ’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power position terms (x, xВі, xвҒө) вҶ’ symmetric restoring force from symmetric potential well
- Even-power position terms (xВІ) in restoring force вҶ’ asymmetric potential / broken symmetry
- Product xВІ*v вҶ’ amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-excited oscillators (van der Pol type)
- Sinusoidal function of position sin(c*x) вҶ’ geometric nonlinearity from angular/pendulum-like systems
- Cosine of time cos(c*t) as additive term вҶ’ external periodic driving force
- Product x*cos(c*t) вҶ’ parametric excitation where system stiffness is modulated in time
- Cubic velocity term vВі вҶ’ Rayleigh-type nonlinear dissipation
- Absence of explicit time dependence вҶ’ autonomous/conservative system; presence suggests driving or parametric effects
- Linear v term with negative coefficient вҶ’ energy dissipation (damping); positive coefficient вҶ’ energy injection (self-excitation)
- Combination of linear and cubic x terms with opposite signs вҶ’ double-well (bistable) potential landscape
